The first provided transformer will be used when writing to\\n91: // the store.\\n92: func NewPrefixTransformers(err error, transformers ...PrefixTransformer) Transformer {\\n93: \\tif err == nil {\\n94: \\t\\terr = fmt.Errorf(\\\"the provided value does not match any of the supported transformers\\\")\\n95: \\t}\\n96: \\treturn &prefixTransformers{\\n97: \\t\\ttransformers: transformers,\\n98: \\t\\terr:          err,\\n99: \\t}\\n100: }\\n101: \\n102: // TransformFromStorage finds the first transformer with a prefix matching the provided data and returns\\n103: // the result of transforming the value.      \\\"keys\\\": [\\n144: \\t\\t\\t//        {\\n145: \\t\\t\\t//          \\\"name\\\": \\\"1\\\",\\n146: \\t\\t\\t//          \\\"secret\\\": \\\"some key 1\\\"\\n147: \\t\\t\\t//        }\\n148: \\t\\t\\t//      ]\\n149: \\t\\t\\t//    }\\n150: \\t\\t\\t//  },\\n151: \\t\\t\\t//\\n152: \\t\\t\\t// The transformers for both aescbc configs share the prefix k8s:enc:aescbc:v1:\\n153: \\t\\t\\t// Additionally, these fields can be used to ensure that the correct transformers are applied to each resource.\\n90: \\t\\t\\t\\t# TYPE apiserver_storage_transformation_operations_total counter\\n91: \\t\\t\\t\\tapiserver_storage_transformation_operations_total{resource=\\\"test\\\",status=\\\"FailedPrecondition\\\",transformation_type=\\\"from_storage\\\",transformer_prefix=\\\"k8s:enc:kms:v1:\\\"} 1\\n92: \\t\\t\\t\\tapiserver_storage_transformation_operations_total{resource=\\\"test\\\",status=\\\"FailedPrecondition\\\",transformation_type=\\\"to_storage\\\",transformer_prefix=\\\"k8s:enc:kms:v1:\\\"} 1\\n93: \\t\\t\\t\\t`,\\n94: \\t\\t\\texpectErr: true,\\n95: \\t\\t},\\n96: \\t\\t{\\n97: \\t\\t\\tdesc:   \\\"internal\\\",\\n98: \\t\\t\\tprefix: NewPrefixTransformers(nil, internalErrTransformer),\\n99: \\t\\t\\tmetrics: []string{\\n100: \\t\\t\\t\\t\\\"apiserver_storage_transformation_operations_total\\\",\\n101: \\t\\t\\t},\\n102: \\t\\t\\twant: `\\n103: \\t\\t\\t\\t# HELP apiserver_storage_transformation_operations_total [ALPHA] Total number of transformations.
